<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>Abstract<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:4.7pt;mso-para-margin-right:.47gd'><span
lang=EN-US>Bitcoin</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>등장과</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이용한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>거래의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>급증은</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기술이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>원장으로서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신뢰</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>할</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만큼</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>충분히</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>안전하다는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>것을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>증명하였다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-2.3pt;mso-para-margin-right:-.23gd'><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기술이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>주목</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>받게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>된</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>주된</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이유는</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기존</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>방식과</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>달리</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신뢰성</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>확보</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>문제에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있어서</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>제</span><span lang=EN-US>3</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>신뢰기관</span><span lang=EN-US> (Trusted Third Party, TTP) </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>제거</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하였다는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>것과</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>모든</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>거래</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>내역이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>네트워크에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>참여하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>참여자들에게</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>분산</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>저장됨으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>내용에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>조작이</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>사실상</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>불가능</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하도록</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>만들었다는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>점이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-2.3pt;mso-para-margin-right:-.23gd'><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기술에서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가장</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>중요한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>핵심</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개념은</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘Decentralization (</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>탈</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>중앙화</span><span lang=EN-US>)’ </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>과</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘Distributed Ledger (</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>분산원장</span><span
lang=EN-US>)’ </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개념이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기존</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>방식은</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하나의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>집중화된</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>중앙</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>서버에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>되고</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>해당</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신뢰는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>중앙서버</span> <span lang=EN-US>(</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>제</span><span lang=EN-US>3</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>신뢰기관</span><span lang=EN-US>) </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>의하여</span> <span lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>보증</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>되는</span><span lang=EN-US>’ </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>방식</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이였다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그러나</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>상에서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>발생한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>거래는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>네트워크에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>참여하는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>참여자들에게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전달되어</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>검증</span><span lang=EN-US>’, ‘</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>합의</span><span lang=EN-US>’</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>되고</span><span
lang=EN-US>, ‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록</span><span lang=EN-US>’ </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>단위로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>묶여</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>순차적</span><span
lang=EN-US>(</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>선형적</span><span lang=EN-US>)</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>연결된다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:4.7pt;mso-para-margin-right:.47gd'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:4.7pt;mso-para-margin-right:.47gd'><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>내역이</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>되는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>크기는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>누적</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>건수가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>증가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>할수록</span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>즉</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>시간이</span> <span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>커질</span> <span

Arial'>수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>밖에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>없으며</span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>네트워크의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>참여자가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전체</span> <span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>관리</span> <span

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>지는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>시점이</span> <span

Arial'>언젠가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>도래함을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의미한다</span><span
lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>즉</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인</span> <span

Arial'>전체를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>저장</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>관리</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>할</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>만큼의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>성능을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갖춘</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>시스템</span><span lang=EN-US>(</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>노드</span><span
lang=EN-US>)</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>점차</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>그</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>줄어</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>상대적으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>소수의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>노드</span> <span

Arial'>집단을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이루게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>될</span> <span

Arial'>그리고</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>크기는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>시간이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>지날수록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>거래의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>누적</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>건수에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>비례하여</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>지속적으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>증가할</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>밖에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>없다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>네트워크에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>참여하는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>노드에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>원장이</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>분산</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>저장</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>관리</span> <span

size</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>또한</span> <span lang=EN-US>Bitcoin </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>현재</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전세계</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>적으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>존재하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>완전</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>노드의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>약</span> <span
lang=EN-US>5,000 ~ 7,000 </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개</span> <span

Arial'>정도의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

Arial'>있다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

Arial'>다수의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>체인으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>분류될</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있음을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의미한다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>N-Dimensional Blockchain – X.Blockchain<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>X.Blockchain </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>은</span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>앞서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>언급한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>전자문서의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>특성을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>반영하여</span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>문서에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>모든</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록</span><span lang=EN-US>(Transaction) </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하나의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>선형적인</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>구조로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>연결하지</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>않고</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>문서</span><span lang=EN-US>’ </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>또는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>준하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>어떤</span> <span lang=EN-US>‘</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기준</span><span lang=EN-US>’ </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>으로</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>분류한다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그리고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기준에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>따라</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>복수의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>체인을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구성</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>함으로서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다차원</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>형태의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>제안한다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>문서</span><span lang=EN-US>’</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하였을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>때</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>각</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서의</span> <span lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>최초</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>생성</span><span lang=EN-US>’ </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>은</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기존</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인과</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>동일한</span> <span

Arial'>선형적인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구조의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기록된다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그러나</span> <span

Arial'>이미</span> <span lang=EN-US>main-chain</span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록된</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>특정</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>발생한</span> <span

Arial'>변경</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>등의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>추가</span> <span

Arial'>기록</span><span lang=EN-US>(Transaction)</span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>은</span><span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이</span> <span

<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>위</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그림은</span> <span
lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>차원</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구조로</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>구성된</span> <span lang=EN-US>X.Blockchain </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>모습이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>앞서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>언급한</span> <span lang=EN-US>‘</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서</span><span lang=EN-US>’</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>를</span> <span
lang=EN-US>main-chain</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>잡았을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>때</span><span
lang=EN-US>, main-chain </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>구성하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>각각의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록</span><span
lang=EN-US>(B<sub>00</sub> ~ B<sub>n0</sub>)</span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>은</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>모두</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신규</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>생성</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>포함하며</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>동시에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>각</span> <span lang=EN-US>sub-chain</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
lang=EN-US>genesis block </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>될</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있다</span><span
lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>예를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>들어</span> <span
lang=EN-US>B<sub>20</sub> </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>생성이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록된</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전자</span> <span

Arial'>문서</span> <span lang=EN-US>E<sub>20</sub> </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이는</span> <span

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>아닌</span><span lang=EN-US>, B<sub>20</sub> </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span lang=EN-US>genesis block </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>으로</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하는</span><span lang=EN-US> sub-chain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>상의</span> <span lang=EN-US>B<sub>21</sub></span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>에</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>된다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>선형적인</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

Arial'>예이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>즉</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서</span> <span lang=EN-US>D<sub>2</sub></span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>필요한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>클라이언트라</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>할지라도</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>사실상</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>불필요한</span> <span
lang=EN-US>D<sub>0</sub>, D<sub>1</sub>, D<sub>3</sub>,</span><span

Arial'>에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록과</span> <span
lang=EN-US>D<sub>0</sub></span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>담은</span> <span

lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그러나</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>으로</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

Arial'>다음과</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>같아진다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>연관성을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갖는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>문서의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>집합이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>분류</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>적용될</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수도</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>있다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>또한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>상황에</span> <span

Arial'>따라서</span> <span lang=EN-US>sub-chain</span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>은</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>또</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다른</span> <span
lang=EN-US>sub-chain</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span
lang=EN-US>main-chain</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>되도록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구성이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가능하다</span><span
lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>토지대장의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>경우</span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>큰</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>범위의</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>지역</span><span lang=EN-US>’</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span lang=EN-US>main-chain</span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기준으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

Arial'>차원</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>X.Blockchain </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>상에서</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>완전노드는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>여기서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>완전</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>노드는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신뢰여부를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>확인해</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>주는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>제</span><span lang=EN-US>3</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>신뢰기관이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>아닌</span> <span
lang=EN-US>‘</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>채굴</span><span lang=EN-US>’</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>수행하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>역할을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>할</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>뿐이다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그러나</span> <span lang=EN-US>X.Blockchain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>각</span><span lang=EN-US> sub-chain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>별로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>채굴</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

Arial'>가능하다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>예를</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>들어</span> <span lang=EN-US>main-chain </span><span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>상의</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록</span> <span lang=EN-US>B<sub>n0</sub> </span><span

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>작업과</span> <span lang=EN-US>sub-chain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>상의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록</span> <span lang=EN-US>B<sub>2m</sub> </span><span

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>작업은</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>서로</span> <span

<span lang=EN-US>B<sub>2m</sub></span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갖지</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>않기</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>때문이다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

Arial'>뒤</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>문서</span> <span

Arial'>그림이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>그러나</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>생성</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

Arial'>의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>변경</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>사항에</span> <span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>작업이</span> <span

style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>작업은</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>각각</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>독립적으로</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>동시</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>진행이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가능하다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>Effectiveness<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>주민등록초본을</span> <span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전자문서화</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하고</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>기술을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>적용</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하여</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>관리</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>상황을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>가정하였을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>때</span><span lang=EN-US>, X.Blockchain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>적용과</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기존</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>적용이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>어떻게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다른가에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>대하여</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>설명한다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구성</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>인구</span> <span
lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>명당</span> <span lang=EN-US>1</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>개의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>초본이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>존재하고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다시</span> <span lang=EN-US>1</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>개의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구성한다고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>가정하였으며</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>해마다</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이동</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>인구수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만큼</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>주민등록초본</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갱신이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>발생하고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>역시</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>하나의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록됨을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가정하였다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한민국의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>총인구는</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>국가통계포털</span><span lang=EN-US>(<a href="http://kosis.kr">http://kosis.kr</a>)
</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>발표에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>따르면</span> <span
lang=EN-US>2015</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>년말</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기준</span> <span
lang=EN-US>51,525,338</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>명</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>인구</span> <span
lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>명당</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>주민등록초본</span><span
lang=EN-US> 1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>부가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>존재하고</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>거주</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>지역을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이동</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>할</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>때</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>마다</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>초본은</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갱신되어야</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>위</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>표의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>데이터에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>따르자면</span><span
lang=EN-US> 2016</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>년</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>해</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>번</span><a
style='mso-footnote-id:ftn7' href="#_ftn7" name="_ftnref7" title=""><span
class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-special-character:
footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>이를</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>선형적인</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인으로</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구성한다면</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>최초</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인은</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>전체</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>인구수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만큼의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록으로</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>구성되고</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>해마다</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>인동</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>인구수</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만큼의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>추가되어야</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>한다</span><span
lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만약</span> <span lang=EN-US>2016</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>년부터</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>적용한다면</span> <span lang=EN-US>2016</span><span

style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록</span><span lang=EN-US> 1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개당</span> <span
lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개의</span> <span lang=EN-US>sub-chain</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>을</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>갖고</span><span lang=EN-US>, sub-chain</span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>당</span> <span lang=EN-US>1.35</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>개</span><a
style='mso-footnote-id:ftn9' href="#_ftn9" name="_ftnref9" title=""><span
class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-special-character:
footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:
"맑은 고딕";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:KO;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>[9]</span></span><![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=EN-US> </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록을</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>갖게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>된다</span><span lang=EN-US>. </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>근거한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>인구</span> <span
lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>명당</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>크기는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>아래와</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>같다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>선형</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>구조의</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록체인과는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>달리</span> <span lang=EN-US>X.Blockchain </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>경우</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>필요한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>데이터에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>선별적</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>관리가</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>가능하다</span><span
lang=EN-US>. </span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만약</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>어떤</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>이유에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의하여</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>특정</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>인구</span> <span lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>백만명에</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>주민등록초본관리</span> <span style='font-family:
"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>등과</span>
<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>같은</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>서비스가</span> <span

Arial'>가능하다는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

Arial'>년동안의</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>변경</span> <span

Arial'>이력에</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>검증을</span> <span

Arial'>위해서</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다음과</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>같다</span><span lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>향후</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>블록체인의</span> <span

Arial'>크기는</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>해마다</span> <span lang=EN-US>1</span><span

Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>대한</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span

Arial'>한해</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>변경</span> <span
style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial'>블록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>크기</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>만큼만</span> <span

Arial'>증가하게</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>다만</span><span lang=EN-US>, </span><span

Arial'>개입</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>없이</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>스스로</span> <span

Arial'>해결</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>할</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;

Arial'>있도록</span> <span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>데</span> <span

mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있다</span><span
lang=EN-US>.</span></p>

style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>의</span><span style='font-size:8.0pt'> <span
lang=EN-US>TPS</span></span><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>는</span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt'> </span><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>약</span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt'> <span lang=EN-US>7 TPS </span></span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>정도를</span><span style='font-size:8.0pt'> </span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>기록하고</span><span style='font-size:8.0pt'> </span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial'>있다</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
8.0pt'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

</div>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn7' href="#_ftnref7"

<span style='font-family:"맑은 고딕",sans-serif;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
